<div style="text-align:center"><div style="width:8.5in;text-align:left;margin-left: auto;margin-right: auto">

<table style="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt;border:0;width:100%" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0">
<tr style="page-break-inside:avoid">
<td style="width:11%;vertical-align:top" align="left"><span style="font-weight:bold">Item&#160;5.02.</span></td>
<td align="left" style="vertical-align:top"> <p style=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;text-align:left">Departure of Directors or Certain Officers; Election of Directors; Appointment of Certain Officers; Compensatory Arrangements of Certain Officers. </p></td></tr></table> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On April&#160;6, 2021, Stephen Kappes notified the Board of Directors (the &#8220;Board&#8221;) of <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> US, Inc. (the &#8220;Company&#8221;) of his decision to resign from the Board and the Nominating and Corporate Governance Committee of the Board, effective immediately. Mr.&#160;Kappes&#8217; resignation is not the result of any disagreement between Mr.&#160;Kappes and the Company or any of its affiliates on any matter relating to the operations, policies or practices of the Company. </p> <p style="font-size:18pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&#160;</p>
<table style="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt;border:0;width:100%" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0">
<tr style="page-break-inside:avoid">
<td style="width:11%;vertical-align:top" align="left"><span style="font-weight:bold">Item&#160;7.01.</span></td>
<td align="left" style="vertical-align:top"> <p style=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;text-align:left">Regulation FD Disclosure </p></td></tr></table> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On April&#160;12, 2021, the Company issued a press release announcing certain determinations regarding director nominees as discussed in Item 8.01 below and the resignation of Mr.&#160;Kappes.&#160;A copy of the press release is attached hereto as Exhibit 99.1 and is incorporated herein by reference. </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The information contained in Item 7.01, including Exhibit 99.1, shall not be deemed &#8220;filed&#8221; for purposes of Section&#160;18 of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934, as amended (the &#8220;Exchange Act&#8221;), or otherwise subject to the liabilities of that section, nor shall it be deemed incorporated by reference in any filing under the Securities Act of 1933, as amended, or the Exchange Act, except as shall be expressly set forth by specific reference in such a filing. </p> <p style="font-size:18pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&#160;</p>
<table style="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt;border:0;width:100%" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0">
<tr style="page-break-inside:avoid">
<td style="width:11%;vertical-align:top" align="left"><span style="font-weight:bold">Item&#160;8.01.</span></td>
<td align="left" style="vertical-align:top"> <p style=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;text-align:left">Other Events. </p></td></tr></table> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On April&#160;12, 2021, the Company announced that the Board has determined to nominate Bavan M. Holloway for election to the Board at the Company&#8217;s 2021 Annual Meeting of Stockholders (the &#8220;Stockholders Meeting&#8221;) to be held on June&#160;3, 2021. After eight years of service on the Board, Lawrence H. Guffey will not be up for <span style="white-space:nowrap">re-election</span> at the Stockholders Meeting. </p> <p style="font-size:18pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&#160;</p>

<DESCRIPTION>EX-99.1
<TEXT>
<HTML><HEAD>
<TITLE>EX-99.1</TITLE>
</HEAD>
 <BODY BGCOLOR="WHITE">


<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right"><B>Exhibit 99.1 </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:22pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>Bavan M. Holloway Nominated to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> US&nbsp;Board of Directors</B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><I>Company Announces Director Lawrence Guffey to Conclude His Term at Annual Meeting; Also Announces Departure of Board Member Stephen
Kappes</I></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>BELLEVUE, Wash. &#151; April&nbsp;12, 2021 &#151;</B><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">&nbsp;T-Mobile</FONT> US, Inc. (NASDAQ: TMUS) today
announced that finance executive Bavan M. Holloway has been nominated to join its board of directors. If elected by stockholders, Holloway is expected to join the board and its Audit Committee after
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#146;s</FONT> annual stockholders meeting on June&nbsp;3, 2021. The company&#146;s other 12 board members will also stand for <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">re-election</FONT> at that annual meeting. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Holloway has over 30 years of broad finance and audit experience in complex and highly regulated business environments. Holloway previously was Vice President
of Corporate Audit for Boeing, among other senior finance roles. She was also previously a Partner at KPMG. Holloway holds a bachelor&#146;s degree in Administration from the University of Tulsa and a master&#146;s degree in Financial Markets and
Trading from the Illinois Institute of Technology. She currently serves on the board for TPI Composites Inc. and the YWCA Seattle/King/Snohomish and previously served on the board of the Special Olympics of Washington.</P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> also shared that board member Lawrence H. Guffey will not seek
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">re-election</FONT> at the annual meeting of stockholders and that board member Stephen Kappes resigned from the board effective April 6th. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;We will welcome Bavan Holloway to our board. I am confident she will be an amazing addition to this talented team of advisors, and we will be lucky to
have her skills and experience join this team,&#148; said Timotheus H&ouml;ttges, Chairman of the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> US Board of Directors. &#147;On behalf of our shareholders and the board, I also want to express my
deep appreciation to Larry and Stephen for all their contributions to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile.</FONT> Larry has served as a director since the public listing of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> in 2013 and has been
a key contributor to the success of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> on our <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Un-carrier</FONT> journey. We will greatly miss his wisdom and steadfast advice. Steve has served on the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> board as our designated security director and has also been a trusted advisor. I wish them both well.&#148; </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;We are incredibly excited to welcome Bavan Holloway to the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> Board of Directors and can&#146;t wait to
tap into her vast knowledge and leadership in auditing and finance as we drive toward executing on our vision to become the best in the world at connecting customers to their world,&#148; said Mike Sievert, CEO of
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile.</FONT> &#147;Bavan&#146;s expertise and diverse perspective will be invaluable as <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> kicks off our next chapter as a supercharged
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Un-carrier.&#148;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Lawrence H. Guffey will continue to serve on the board until the upcoming annual meeting. Guffey
has served on <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#146;s</FONT> board of directors since April 2013 and is a member of the Section&nbsp;16 Subcommittee of the Compensation Committee, the Executive Committee, and the Transaction Committee. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Kappes became a member of the board on April&nbsp;1, 2020 and had previously served as a Sprint director since May 2018 and was a member of the Nominating and
Corporate Governance Committee.</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"># # # </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>About <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B></B><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> U.S. Inc.&nbsp;(NASDAQ: TMUS) is America&#146;s supercharged
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Un-carrier,</FONT> delivering an advanced 4G LTE and transformative nationwide 5G network that will offer reliable connectivity for all. <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#146;s</FONT> customers benefit from
its unmatched combination of value and quality, unwavering obsession with offering them the best possible service experience and undisputable drive for disruption that creates competition and innovation in wireless and beyond. Based in Bellevue,
Wash., <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> provides services through its subsidiaries and operates its flagship brands, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile,</FONT> Metro by <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> and
Sprint. For more information please visit: <U><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">https://www.t-mobile.com</FONT></U>.</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Media Contact </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B></B><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> US, Inc. Media Relations </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">MediaRelations@t-mobile.com</FONT></U></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Investor Relations Contact </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> US, Inc. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">investor.relations@t-mobile.com</FONT> </U></P>
